<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">

          function GetNode() { return external.SnapinScopeObject(); }

          var node;
		  var tables = [];
		  
		  var floatCaptionBox = document.createElement("DIV");
			var classHideCaption = "table_floatcaption_wrap";
			var classShowCaption = "table_floatcaption_wrap active";
			floatCaptionBox.className = classHideCaption;
			floatCaptionBox.id = "floatCaptionBox";

          function OnLoad() {

			  try {
			  node = GetNode();
			  cmd1.innerText = node.GetCounter("cmd1");
			  cmd2.innerText = node.GetCounter("cmd2");
			  cmd3.innerText = node.GetCounter("cmd3");
			  cmd4.innerText = node.GetCounter("cmd4");
			  cmd5.innerText = node.GetCounter("cmd5");
			  } catch(err) {}

			  try { EventsRetranslator.ConnectTo(GetNode()) }
			  catch(err) {}
		  
		  
		    document.body.appendChild(floatCaptionBox);
            getTablesArr();


            window.onscroll = function() {
                renderFloatCaption();
            }

            window.onresize = function() {
                getTablesArr();
                renderFloatCaption();
            }
		  
		  
          }
		  
		  
		  
			function getTablesArr() {
				var allTables = document.getElementsByTagName("TABLE");

				tables = [];

				for(var i=0, length = allTables.length; i < length; i++) {
					
					if (allTables[i].className.indexOf("DATA_TABLE") != -1) {						
						var tableObj = {};

						var originalCaptionTR = allTables[i].getElementsByTagName("TR")[0];
						var originalCaptionTD_arr = originalCaptionTR.getElementsByTagName("TD");

						var floatCaptionTable = document.createElement("TABLE");
						var cloneTR = originalCaptionTR.cloneNode(true);

						for (var y = 0, length_clone = cloneTR.getElementsByTagName("TD").length; y < length_clone; y++) {
							if (originalCaptionTD_arr[y].offsetWidth > 0) {
								cloneTR.getElementsByTagName("TD")[y].style.width = originalCaptionTD_arr[y].offsetWidth - 17 + "px";
							}
						}

						floatCaptionTable.className = "table_floatcaption";
						floatCaptionTable.appendChild(cloneTR);

						tableObj.el = allTables[i];
						tableObj.height = allTables[i].offsetHeight;
						tableObj.fixedCaption = floatCaptionTable;
						tables.push(tableObj);
						
						
						function resolveData(attr) {
						
							var event = event || window.event							
							var target = event.target || event.srcElement;
							
							if(typeof target === "undefined") {									
								return false;
							}
							
							var targetAttr = target.getAttribute(attr);								
							result = targetAttr ? targetAttr : '';								
							return result;
						}
						
						allTables[i].onclick = function tableClick(event) {						
							
							switch (resolveData('data-function')) {
							
							  case 'f':
							  
								F(
									resolveData('data-df_name'),
									resolveData('data-arg_val'),
									resolveData('data-hst'),
									resolveData('data-srvInst'),
									resolveData('data-srvName')
								);
								
								break;
								
								
							  case 'sort':
							  	
								
								
								Sort(
									resolveData('data-issum') == "true" ? true : false, 
									resolveData('data-name'), 
									resolveData('data-order')
								);
								
								break;							  
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}


			function renderFloatCaption() {
				var floatCaptionBox = document.getElementById("floatCaptionBox");
				var obj = determineCurrentTable();
				

				if (obj) {					
					if(floatCaptionBox.children[0] && (floatCaptionBox.children[0].tagName == "TABLE")) {						
						floatCaptionBox.removeChild(floatCaptionBox.children[0]);					
					}
					floatCaptionBox.appendChild(obj.fixedCaption);					
					showFloatCaption();
					correctLeftPos();
				}
				else {
					hideFloatCaption();
				}
			}

			function showFloatCaption() {
				floatCaptionBox.className = classShowCaption;
			}

			function hideFloatCaption() {
				floatCaptionBox.className = classHideCaption;				
			}

			function correctLeftPos() {
				var scrollLeft = document.documentElement ? document.documentElement.scrollLeft : document.body.scrollLeft;
				floatCaptionBox.style.left = (-1 * (scrollLeft - 20)) + "px";				
			}

			function determineCurrentTable() {
				for (var i = 0, length = tables.length; i < length; i++) {
					var coordinates = tables[i].el.getBoundingClientRect();
					
					if ((coordinates.top < 0) && (0 < (coordinates.top + tables[i].height))) {						
						return tables[i];
					}
				}
				hideFloatCaption();
				return null;
			}





		  


          function Print() {
          document.execCommand('Print')
          }

          function Sort(isSummary, columnName, curOrder) {
          var order = "a";
          if (curOrder > 0) order = "d";
		  
          node.ExecuteCommand2(isSummary?"SortSum":"SortDet", columnName, order);
          }

          function F(sFieldName, sValue, hosts, srvinst, srvname) 
		  {
			  var cmdName = "InteractiveFilter";
			  switch(hosts){
				case "0": cmdName = "InteractiveFilter"; break;
				case "1": cmdName = "InteractiveQuery"; break;
				case "2": cmdName = "AdaptiveSecurityDetects"; break;
			  }

			  if (srvinst == "")
				node.ExecuteCommand2(cmdName, sFieldName, sValue);
			  else
				node.ExecuteCommand4(cmdName, sFieldName, sValue, srvinst, srvname);
          }

          var g_bShowMaster = true;

          function ToggleMaster() {
          g_bShowMaster = !g_bShowMaster;

          if (g_bShowMaster)
          document.getElementById("Master").style.display = "inline";
          else
          document.getElementById("Master").style.display = "none";
          }

          var g_bShowSlaves = true;

          function ToggleSlaves() {
          g_bShowSlaves = !g_bShowSlaves;

          if (g_bShowSlaves)
          document.getElementById("Slaves").style.display = "inline";
          else
          document.getElementById("Slaves").style.display = "none";
          }

          var g_bShowDetails = false;

          function ToggleDetails() {
          g_bShowDetails = !g_bShowDetails;

          if (g_bShowDetails)
          document.getElementById("Details").style.display = "inline";
          else
          document.getElementById("Details").style.display = "none";
          }

          function ToggleSlaveDetails(table) {
          if (document.getElementById(table).style.display == "inline")
          document.getElementById(table).style.display = "none";
          else
          document.getElementById(table).style.display = "inline";
          }

          function OnNavigate(page) {
          window.navigate(page);
          }

          function OnUnload() {
          try {
          EventsRetranslator.DisconnectFrom(GetNode());
          } catch(err){}
          }

          window.onload = OnLoad;
          window.onunload = OnUnload;

        </script><script language="JavaScript" FOR="EventsRetranslator" EVENT="NHEvent_Navigate(page)">
            OnNavigate(page);
          </script><style type="text/css">

              display: none
            }
